msg:The design of the hotel and room is fantastic! I really like the look of everything. But there are several little practical things that really make for an unpleasant experience. It's not easy to get a good night's sleep. The light switches glow in the dark which is cool when awake but not nice for sleeping. The curtains don't block out the light very well. There are at least 4 helicopters outside of the hotel causing a lot of noise from very early in the morning. The noise doesn't end. Not very pleasant. The water in the shower isn't very warm. But the shower does look very nice. I would think very carefully about staying here if a person needs to relax and sleep well. There are 33 floors. The 3 elevators are extremely frustrating. While waiting for a very long time, the elevator automatically cancels itself while I wait for an elevator. I waited about 15 minutes. Each time I have to push the button again because it cancels automatically. I had to do this 5 times just to get an elevator to get down. The alternative is to walk down the stairs from the 21st floor where I was. So many small problems. Also it's easy to replace the rusty mirror in the bathroom. The basin is also mouldy. The master light switch very frustratingly cancels the electric plugs as well. So you can't charge your devices or use the bedside plugs while the lights are off. Surely these things need to be addressed and fixed. The place really looks nice and has a lot of potential.

At least put a small table for me to put my mobile phone and bath towel. The bathtub is dusty outdoors, so I asked the hotel for a bath bag. I am really convinced. This bath bag is too bad. There is no packaging. It is just a plastic sheet. At least give a bath bag with independent packaging and fixed bag.
The method of using the bathroom shower is almost transparent. If you don't look carefully, you can't see it clearly. Not everyone has used the same brand and model of shower, especially this one is different from the style and function used by the public. If it is a slightly older customer who has not used the same shower, it is estimated that it will be very difficult to use.
The room number marked on the phone in the room is different from the actual room number, which caused me to keep saying the wrong room number when communicating with the hotel front desk.
At one o'clock in the morning, several people were talking loudly at the door, which woke me up from my sleep. It may be because my room is opposite the elevator. Those people kept chatting at my door for at least 15 minutes. Later, I called the front desk to let the staff come up to deal with it before they quieted down. The entire hotel room facilities are too old, and the service is not up to par. The hotel has a shuttle bus to pick up passengers on the island, which was not informed to me when I checked in.

1. Location: Located in the seaside in the urban area - Sanya Bay, the island also has a wedding photography base, water sports such as yachts and motorboats, helicopter sightseeing and Xisha cruises, so the flow of people is large, if you enter and leave Phoenix Island, it is for the hotel Privacy needs to be improved. 2. Environmental facilities: If the entire Phoenix Island is regarded as the scope of the hotel, it is indeed very huge. First of all, the only way to enter and leave the island is a two-way cross-sea bridge, which can be said to be a flower road (Sanya City Flower Triangle). Mei), the slope is relatively large, entering from outside the island, at a certain angle, you can enjoy the visual enjoyment of the scenery in the island slowly emerging from the sea level. After getting off the bridge, the first roundabout is divided into two forks, and the right turn is Helicopter sightseeing and wedding photography, yachts out to sea, wakes out of waves, etc. üåä Ronin's distribution center, go to the left to go to the cruise line and the hotel direction. Since there is a wharf on the island, there is a certain amount of noise. Partners who need a quiet environment will still have a certain impact. I There are only 8 parking spaces on the ground in the hotel area, and the security will guide you to the underground garage for parking. The entrances are all guarded, and you need to scan the location code to enter.

3. Service: When entering the lobby, the staff who have eye contact will wave hello üôã Greetings, the tall and handsome little brother will also take the initiative to help with luggage üß≥, and the ladies at the front desk are also tall and beautiful women ü•∞, warm introduction Check-in matters and the hotel's basic service facilities, since the lobby is open without air conditioning, the lady will also send a small bottle of mineral water and an old popsicle to relieve the heat. Travel strategies are provided, and the room service responds quickly, basically within 5-10 minutes. The overall service experience is that the staff has a sense of ownership and does have the feeling of being a guest, which proves that the hotel management attaches great importance to the guest experience and is worthy of the landmark. called

4. Hygiene: Generally, there is no problem. The places that can be in direct contact with the human body are clean and hygienic. The hygiene of public areas is also frequently cleaned. I ordered takeout several times and put it at the door after use, all within half an hour. I took it away, and didn't even bother to remind it.

5. Catering: The dining experience is not comprehensive due to the fact that most of them are eating out. The breakfast category is quite rich. The scenery of the sky lounge is really wow, suitable for punching in and taking picturesüì∑

Overall, the cost-effectiveness is high. It is worth coming to Sanya to check in at this landmark. Friends, red duck! ü´°
